## âœ¨ Literal Explanation (EN)

Toadgod shares an operational and philosophical update:

- **Scaling success**: A new solution tested successfully, adding 15,000 new $TOBY holders â€” small but meaningful progress.
- **Base congestion**: Current conditions create high execution fees (50x normal), so Toadgod will adjust timing strategically.
- **Final byÅdÅ shugi system**: For remaining airdrops, a "fairness principle system" introducing a reduction in $TOBY distribution.
